name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior queen Room
info:Stayed in August 2022
info:Couples
info:1 Review
rating:3.5
posted:Posted August 19, 2022
msg:I had a nice staycation at the Four Points by Sheraton.  I was happy that they allowed foreigners as many hotels in Beijing are not taking foreigners since the Pandemic.  The location was ok as it was in the area as my university, and I did not want to go far from campus.  The staff were generally friendly and accommodating, and there was always an English-speaking staff member at reception on duty.  All you must do is ask for an English-speaking staff member.  There is a lounge area where you can order snacks and drinks (this is also the same menu for room service). By the way you must request for the room service menu directly from reception and they will send someone to your room to take the order.  There is also the option to pre-order breakfast to have in the room each evening.  There is a traditional Chinese Tea House on the premises for any who are looking for some cultural emersion.  There is also a Chinese barbeque right outside the hotel and you can charge the bill to your room, which I found convenient.  The gym is small but has most equipment and the pool is indoor.  However, it is also used for swimming classes for kids which is inconvenient.  Too many children and too much noise.  The breakfast was nice. A mixture of Chinese and Western cuisine.  Dinner is buffet and a la carte.  The room was clean and comfortable and quiet.  The spa was unfortunately closed.  Overall, I had a good experience and would recommend it for the price point it has.
